commit 41a3fc8885eaf92dc9093f9e63fe26383f187d44
Merge: 7901bc4 8a7377a
Author: Josef Cacek <josef.cacek@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 29 13:20:05 2018 +0300

    Merge pull request #17 from vittala/default-rights
    
    When cmd line encrypting, allow permission to actions by default.

commit 8a7377ac7ef0bb1eda34a755e22616f49abcc2c8
Author: Vittal Aithal <v@aithal.org>
Date:   Wed Jan 24 11:17:41 2018 +0000

    When cmd line encrypting, allow permission to actions by default.
    
    At the moment, when a document is encrypted, all the rights
    get turned off (e.g. copy). This means options like the
    --disable-copy are meaningless. This change enables these
    rights by default, and only disables them if the appropriate
    disable options are set.

6	12	src/net/sf/jsignpdf/SignerOptionsFromCmdLine.java

commit 68e09ea5c082958e400ac6ead6468d2a7177045b
Author: Vaclav Slavik <vslavik@gmail.com>
Date:   Sat Aug 31 12:12:07 2013 +0200

    Make the OCSP verification more robust.
    
    Previous code relied on on having certificates from getCertificates() in
    certain order, even though the documentation said the array is "in no
    particular order".
    
    Instead, use getSignCertificateChain(), which is guaranteed to return
    ordered chain starting with the issuer.
